<script>
/* ======================================================================
 * FCA module parsers — Huntsville BCM & Yazaki FCM
 * Offsets verified from: 2017 LX BCM (68525720AA), 2016 LD BCM (68277389AC),
 *                         two different Yazaki FCM RFHUB dumps
 * ====================================================================== */

const VIN_RE = /[12345][A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9][A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9][A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9]{14}/;
const VIN_CHAR_RE = /^[A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9]$/;

/* ---- BCM (Huntsville Continental) ---- */
/*
 * BCM stores VIN as plain ASCII in 4 redundant slots.
 * Slot layout: 17 bytes of ASCII VIN preceded by "00 46 XX 00" marker
 *              where XX is the slot type (46, 56, 57, 52).
 * VIN slot offsets VARY by BCM variant:
 *   68525720 family: 0x5308, 0x5328, 0x5348, 0x5368  (2014-2015 LX)
 *   68277389 family: 0x1308, 0x1328, 0x1348, 0x1368  (2015-2017 LX)
 * Strategy: search for any 17-byte ASCII run that looks like a VIN
 *           AND is preceded by the 46-46-00 marker pattern.
 */
function crc16Ccitt(data, init = 0xFFFF, poly = 0x1021) {
  let c = init;
  for (const b of data) {
    c ^= b << 8;
    for (let j = 0; j < 8; j++) {
      c = (c & 0x8000) ? (((c << 1) ^ poly) & 0xFFFF) : ((c << 1) & 0xFFFF);
    }
  }
  return c & 0xFFFF;
}

function parseBcm(bytes) {
  const result = {
    ok: false,
    kind: 'BCM',
    size: bytes.length,
    vinSlots: [],
    vin: null,
    vinConsistent: false,
    partNumbers: [],
    supplierSerial: null,
    magic: null,
    magicOffsets: [],
    sequenceNumbers: [],
  };

  // Check FEE1000 magic
  const magic = new TextEncoder().encode('FEE1000');
  for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length - magic.length; i++) {
    let match = true;
    for (let j = 0; j < magic.length; j++) if (bytes[i+j] !== magic[j]) { match = false; break; }
    if (match) {
      result.magicOffsets.push(i);
      if (i >= 2) {
        const seq = (bytes[i-2] << 8) | bytes[i-1];
        result.sequenceNumbers.push({offset: i-2, seq: seq});
      }
    }
  }
  result.magic = result.magicOffsets.length > 0;

  // Scan for VIN slots using marker pattern "00 46 <XX> 00 <17 ASCII VIN bytes>"
  // XX in {0x46, 0x52, 0x53, 0x56, 0x57} — all observed slot types
  const slotTypes = [0x46, 0x52, 0x53, 0x56, 0x57];
  for (let i = 0; i < bytes.length - 21; i++) {
    if (bytes[i] !== 0x00 || bytes[i+1] !== 0x46) continue;
    if (!slotTypes.includes(bytes[i+2])) continue;
    if (bytes[i+3] !== 0x00) continue;
    // Try to read 17 ASCII bytes after the marker
    const vinStart = i + 4;
    if (vinStart + 17 > bytes.length) continue;
    let candidate = '';
    let valid = true;
    for (let k = 0; k < 17; k++) {
      const b = bytes[vinStart + k];
      if (b < 0x20 || b > 0x7E) { valid = false; break; }
      candidate += String.fromCharCode(b);
    }
    if (!valid) continue;
    if (!VIN_RE.test(candidate)) continue;
    // Validate VIN CRC-16/CCITT at offset +17, +18 (big-endian)
    let storedCrc = null, computedCrc = null, crcOk = null;
    if (vinStart + 19 <= bytes.length) {
      storedCrc = (bytes[vinStart + 17] << 8) | bytes[vinStart + 18];
      const vinByteArray = bytes.slice(vinStart, vinStart + 17);
      computedCrc = crc16Ccitt(vinByteArray);
      crcOk = storedCrc === computedCrc;
    }
    result.vinSlots.push({
      offset: vinStart,
      markerOffset: i,
      slotType: bytes[i+2],
      vin: candidate,
      storedCrc,
      computedCrc,
      crcOk,
    });
  }

  if (result.vinSlots.length > 0) {
    const vins = new Set(result.vinSlots.map(s => s.vin));
    result.vin = result.vinSlots[0].vin;
    result.vinConsistent = vins.size === 1;
  }

  // Look for 8-char Mopar part numbers: 5 digits + 3 alnum typically, or 8-digit
  // Simple scan for "68XXXXXX" patterns — all Mopar FCA part numbers start with 68 or 56/05/etc
  const pnRE = /68\d{6}/g;
  const text = new TextDecoder('ascii').decode(bytes);
  const partsSet = new Set();
  let m;
  while ((m = pnRE.exec(text)) !== null) partsSet.add(m[0]);
  result.partNumbers = Array.from(partsSet);

  // Supplier serial: look for TYHxxxxx or similar prefix at isolated positions
  const supplierRE = /TY[A-Z]\d{5}/g;
  while ((m = supplierRE.exec(text)) !== null) { result.supplierSerial = m[0]; break; }

  result.ok = result.vin !== null;
  return result;
}

/* ---- RFHUB (Yazaki FCM Gen 2) ---- */
/*
 * RFHUB stores VIN BYTE-REVERSED at 4 redundant slots:
 *   0x0EA5, 0x0EB9, 0x0ECD, 0x0EE1 — each 17 bytes, followed by "DB 01" trailer
 * SEC16 (18 bytes) stored at:
 *   0x0226 and 0x023A — primary + mirror slot, should be byte-identical when paired
 * Key fob slots: 0x08C0-0x0A60 region, 16 bytes each, padded with 0x50/0x5A when empty
 */
function parseRfh(bytes) {
  const result = {
    ok: false,
    kind: 'RFHUB',
    size: bytes.length,
    vinSlots: [],
    vin: null,
    vinConsistent: false,
    sec16Slot1: null,
    sec16Slot2: null,
    sec16Match: false,
    sec16Virgin: false,
    partNumbers: [],
    internalSerial: null,
    keyCount: 0,
  };

  const VIN_OFFSETS = [0x0EA5, 0x0EB9, 0x0ECD, 0x0EE1];
  for (const off of VIN_OFFSETS) {
    if (off + 17 > bytes.length) continue;
    const slice = bytes.slice(off, off + 17);
    // Reverse bytes to get forward VIN
    const reversed = new Uint8Array(17);
    for (let i = 0; i < 17; i++) reversed[i] = slice[16 - i];
    let candidate = '';
    let valid = true;
    for (let k = 0; k < 17; k++) {
      const b = reversed[k];
      if (b < 0x20 || b > 0x7E) { valid = false; break; }
      candidate += String.fromCharCode(b);
    }
    if (!valid) continue;
    if (!VIN_RE.test(candidate)) continue;
    // Validate VIN checksum at offset +17
    let storedChk = null, computedChk = null, chkOk = null, sumByte = null;
    if (off + 18 <= bytes.length) {
      storedChk = bytes[off + 17];
      sumByte = 0;
      for (const b of slice) sumByte = (sumByte + b) & 0xFF;
      computedChk = (0xF9 - sumByte) & 0xFF;
      chkOk = storedChk === computedChk;
    }
    result.vinSlots.push({ offset: off, vin: candidate, rawReversed: slice,
                           storedChk, computedChk, chkOk, sumByte });
  }

  if (result.vinSlots.length > 0) {
    const vins = new Set(result.vinSlots.map(s => s.vin));
    result.vin = result.vinSlots[0].vin;
    result.vinConsistent = vins.size === 1;
  }

  // SEC16 — 18 bytes at 0x0226 and 0x023A
  if (bytes.length >= 0x0226 + 18) {
    result.sec16Slot1 = bytes.slice(0x0226, 0x0226 + 18);
  }
  if (bytes.length >= 0x023A + 18) {
    result.sec16Slot2 = bytes.slice(0x023A, 0x023A + 18);
  }
  if (result.sec16Slot1 && result.sec16Slot2) {
    result.sec16Match = true;
    for (let i = 0; i < 18; i++) {
      if (result.sec16Slot1[i] !== result.sec16Slot2[i]) { result.sec16Match = false; break; }
    }
    // Virgin = both slots all 0xFF
    const allFF = arr => Array.from(arr).every(b => b === 0xFF);
    result.sec16Virgin = allFF(result.sec16Slot1) && allFF(result.sec16Slot2);
  }

  // Detect 2020+ extended SEC16 at 0x0500 (AA 55 magic)
  result.extendedSec16 = null;
  if (bytes.length >= 0x0538 && bytes[0x0500] === 0xAA && bytes[0x0501] === 0x55) {
    const slot1 = bytes.slice(0x050E, 0x050E + 16);
    const slot2 = bytes.slice(0x0522, 0x0522 + 16);
    let match = true;
    for (let i = 0; i < 16; i++) { if (slot1[i] !== slot2[i]) { match = false; break; } }
    const allFF = a => Array.from(a).every(b => b === 0xFF);
    result.extendedSec16 = {
      present: true,
      slot1, slot2, match,
      virgin: allFF(slot1) && allFF(slot2),
    };
  }

  // Part numbers — search for "AA30712804", "BAxxxxxxxx" patterns
  const text = new TextDecoder('ascii').decode(bytes);
  const pnRE = /(?:AA\d{8}|BA\d{8})/g;
  const partsSet = new Set();
  let m;
  while ((m = pnRE.exec(text)) !== null) partsSet.add(m[0]);
  result.partNumbers = Array.from(partsSet);

  // Internal serial
  const serialRE = /\d{4}[A-Z]\d{3,4}[A-Z]{2}\d{2}[A-Z]/g;
  while ((m = serialRE.exec(text)) !== null) { result.internalSerial = m[0]; break; }

  // Count programmed keys — fob slots at ~0x08C0-0x0A60, 16-byte stride
  // An empty slot is filled with 0x50 0x50 0x50 0x50 0x50 pattern
  const KEY_SLOT_START = 0x08C0;
  const KEY_SLOT_END = 0x0A60;
  const KEY_SLOT_STRIDE = 48;  // approximate stride for Yazaki fob records
  // We'll count slots that contain non-0x50/0x5A/0xFF data in their first 8 bytes
  for (let off = KEY_SLOT_START; off < KEY_SLOT_END && off + 16 < bytes.length; off += KEY_SLOT_STRIDE) {
    const head = bytes.slice(off, off + 8);
    const fill = Array.from(head).every(b => b === 0x50 || b === 0x5A || b === 0xFF);
    if (!fill) result.keyCount++;
  }

  result.ok = result.vin !== null;
  return result;
}

/* ---- Sync operations ---- */

function writeBcmVin(bytes, newVin) {
  /*
   * Overwrites all 4 VIN slots in the BCM with the new VIN (ASCII forward) AND
   * recomputes the 2-byte CRC-16/CCITT (big-endian) stored immediately after each VIN.
   * Verified via comparison of factory GH214845 (CRC 0x0D7F) and ImmoVin-edited
   * FH857853 (CRC 0x74B0) — ImmoVin recomputes correctly, so do we.
   */
  const out = new Uint8Array(bytes);
  if (newVin.length !== 17) throw new Error('VIN must be 17 chars');
  const slotTypes = [0x46, 0x52, 0x53, 0x56, 0x57];
  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const newVinBytes = encoder.encode(newVin);
  const newCrc = crc16Ccitt(newVinBytes);
  const crcHi = (newCrc >> 8) & 0xFF, crcLo = newCrc & 0xFF;

  let patched = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < out.length - 21; i++) {
    if (out[i] !== 0x00 || out[i+1] !== 0x46) continue;
    if (!slotTypes.includes(out[i+2])) continue;
    if (out[i+3] !== 0x00) continue;
    const vinStart = i + 4;
    if (vinStart + 19 > out.length) continue;
    // Check if this slot currently holds a VIN-looking value
    let curr = '';
    let valid = true;
    for (let k = 0; k < 17; k++) {
      const b = out[vinStart + k];
      if (b < 0x20 || b > 0x7E) { valid = false; break; }
      curr += String.fromCharCode(b);
    }
    if (!valid || !VIN_RE.test(curr)) continue;
    for (let k = 0; k < 17; k++) out[vinStart + k] = newVinBytes[k];
    // Recompute CRC-16/CCITT stored BE at vinStart+17, vinStart+18
    out[vinStart + 17] = crcHi;
    out[vinStart + 18] = crcLo;
    patched++;
  }
  return { bytes: out, patched, crc: newCrc };
}

function writeRfhVin(bytes, newVin, virginize) {
  /*
   * Overwrites all 4 VIN slots in the RFHUB with the new VIN (byte-reversed)
   * and recomputes the 1-byte VIN checksum stored at the 18th byte of each slot.
   * Formula: chk = (0xF9 - sum(reversed VIN bytes)) & 0xFF
   * Verified across 2015-2020 LX dumps (FH796320, GH214845, FH857853, FH795771, KH728648).
   *
   * If virginize=true:
   *   - wipes legacy SEC16 at 0x0226 and 0x023A (18 bytes each) — present on all dumps
   *   - detects 2020+ extended SEC16 at 0x0500 (AA 55 magic) and wipes 0x0500-0x0537
   *     (54 bytes total: 14-byte header + 2 × 20-byte paired blocks)
   */
  const out = new Uint8Array(bytes);
  if (newVin.length !== 17) throw new Error('VIN must be 17 chars');
  const VIN_OFFSETS = [0x0EA5, 0x0EB9, 0x0ECD, 0x0EE1];
  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const forwardBytes = encoder.encode(newVin);
  const reversedBytes = new Uint8Array(17);
  for (let i = 0; i < 17; i++) reversedBytes[i] = forwardBytes[16 - i];
  let sum = 0;
  for (const b of reversedBytes) sum = (sum + b) & 0xFF;
  const chk = (0xF9 - sum) & 0xFF;

  let patched = 0;
  for (const off of VIN_OFFSETS) {
    if (off + 18 > out.length) continue;
    for (let k = 0; k < 17; k++) out[off + k] = reversedBytes[k];
    out[off + 17] = chk;
    patched++;
  }

  let sec16Wiped = 0;
  let extendedWiped = false;
  if (virginize) {
    // Legacy SEC16 (all generations)
    for (const secOff of [0x0226, 0x023A]) {
      if (secOff + 18 > out.length) continue;
      for (let k = 0; k < 18; k++) out[secOff + k] = 0xFF;
      sec16Wiped++;
    }
    // 2020+ extended SEC16: detect AA 55 magic at 0x0500
    if (out.length >= 0x0538 && out[0x0500] === 0xAA && out[0x0501] === 0x55) {
      for (let k = 0x0500; k < 0x0538; k++) out[k] = 0xFF;
      extendedWiped = true;
    }
  }

  return { bytes: out, patched, sec16Wiped, extendedWiped, chk };
}

/* ======================================================================
 * UI
 * ====================================================================== */

const state = {
  bcm: { file: null, bytes: null, parsed: null },
  rfh: { file: null, bytes: null, parsed: null },
};

function $(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
function hex(n, w=4) { return n.toString(16).toUpperCase().padStart(w, '0'); }
function bytesToHex(bytes) { return Array.from(bytes).map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2,'0').toUpperCase()).join(''); }

function log(msg, level='info') {
  const el = $('log');
  const ts = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-GB', { hour12: false });
  const div = document.createElement('div');
  div.className = 'line';
  div.innerHTML = `<span class="ts">${ts}</span><span class="${level}">${msg}</span>`;
  el.appendChild(div);
  el.scrollTop = el.scrollHeight;
}

function setupDrop(dropId, fileId, kind) {
  const drop = $(dropId);
  const input = $(fileId);
  drop.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
    if (e.target.tagName !== 'INPUT') input.click();
  });
  drop.addEventListener('dragover', e => { e.preventDefault(); drop.classList.add('over'); });
  drop.addEventListener('dragleave', e => { drop.classList.remove('over'); });
  drop.addEventListener('drop', e => {
    e.preventDefault();
    drop.classList.remove('over');
    if (e.dataTransfer.files.length > 0) handleFile(kind, e.dataTransfer.files[0]);
  });
  input.addEventListener('change', e => {
    if (e.target.files.length > 0) handleFile(kind, e.target.files[0]);
  });
}

async function handleFile(kind, file) {
  const buf = await file.arrayBuffer();
  const bytes = new Uint8Array(buf);
  const parsed = kind === 'bcm' ? parseBcm(bytes) : parseRfh(bytes);

  state[kind].file = file;
  state[kind].bytes = bytes;
  state[kind].parsed = parsed;

  const fnameEl = $(kind === 'bcm' ? 'fnameBcm' : 'fnameRfh');
  fnameEl.textContent = `${file.name} · ${bytes.length} bytes`;
  $(kind === 'bcm' ? 'dropBcm' : 'dropRfh').classList.add('loaded');

  log(`Loaded ${kind.toUpperCase()}: ${file.name} (${bytes.length} bytes)`, 'info');
  if (parsed.ok) {
    log(`  ${kind.toUpperCase()} VIN: ${parsed.vin}`, 'ok');
  } else {
    log(`  ${kind.toUpperCase()}: no VIN parsed — check file type`, 'err');
  }

  updateUI();
}

function statusBadge(parsed, kind) {
  if (!parsed || !parsed.ok) return { label: 'NO VIN', cls: 'err' };
  if (!parsed.vinConsistent) return { label: 'VIN SLOTS INCONSISTENT', cls: 'warn' };
  if (kind === 'rfh' && !parsed.sec16Match && !parsed.sec16Virgin) return { label: 'SEC16 MISMATCH', cls: 'warn' };
  if (kind === 'rfh' && parsed.sec16Virgin) return { label: 'SEC16 VIRGIN', cls: 'warn' };
  return { label: 'READY', cls: 'ok' };
}

function renderModCard(parsed, kind) {
  if (!parsed) return '';
  const s = statusBadge(parsed, kind);
  const title = kind === 'bcm' ? '🧠 BCM · MPC5606B' : '🔑 RFHUB · Yazaki FCM';
  let body = '';

  body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Stored VIN</div><div class="v vin">${parsed.vin || '<span class="muted">none</span>'}</div></div>`;
  body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">VIN slots</div><div class="v">${parsed.vinSlots.length} / 4 ${parsed.vinConsistent ? '· all match' : '· MISMATCH'}</div></div>`;
  body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Size</div><div class="v">${parsed.size} bytes (0x${hex(parsed.size,4)})</div></div>`;

  // CRC/checksum status summary
  if (kind === 'bcm' && parsed.vinSlots.length > 0) {
    const allOk = parsed.vinSlots.every(s => s.crcOk);
    const crcValue = parsed.vinSlots[0].computedCrc;
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">VIN CRC-16</div><div class="v">0x${(crcValue ?? 0).toString(16).toUpperCase().padStart(4,'0')} (CCITT/BE) · ${allOk ? '✓ all slots valid' : '✗ mismatch detected'}</div></div>`;
  }
  if (kind === 'rfh' && parsed.vinSlots.length > 0) {
    const allOk = parsed.vinSlots.every(s => s.chkOk);
    const chkValue = parsed.vinSlots[0].computedChk;
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">VIN checksum</div><div class="v">0x${(chkValue ?? 0).toString(16).toUpperCase().padStart(2,'0')} · ${allOk ? '✓ all slots valid' : '⚠ mismatch (older variant?)'}</div></div>`;
  }

  if (kind === 'bcm') {
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Part numbers</div><div class="v">${parsed.partNumbers.length ? parsed.partNumbers.join(', ') : '<span class="muted">none</span>'}</div></div>`;
    if (parsed.supplierSerial) body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Supplier serial</div><div class="v">${parsed.supplierSerial}</div></div>`;
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">DFLASH magic</div><div class="v">${parsed.magic ? 'FEE1000 @ ' + parsed.magicOffsets.map(o=>'0x'+hex(o,4)).join(', ') : '<span class="muted">not found</span>'}</div></div>`;
    if (parsed.sequenceNumbers.length) {
      const seqs = parsed.sequenceNumbers.map(s => `${s.seq}`).join(' / ');
      body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">DFLASH seq</div><div class="v">${seqs}</div></div>`;
    }
  } else {
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Part numbers</div><div class="v">${parsed.partNumbers.length ? parsed.partNumbers.join(', ') : '<span class="muted">none</span>'}</div></div>`;
    if (parsed.internalSerial) body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Serial</div><div class="v">${parsed.internalSerial}</div></div>`;
    const sec1Hex = parsed.sec16Slot1 ? bytesToHex(parsed.sec16Slot1) : '';
    const sec2Hex = parsed.sec16Slot2 ? bytesToHex(parsed.sec16Slot2) : '';
    const sec16Status = parsed.sec16Virgin ? 'VIRGIN (all FF)' : parsed.sec16Match ? 'MATCH' : 'MISMATCH';
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">SEC16 (legacy) slot 1 @ 0x0226</div><div class="v">${sec1Hex.slice(0,36)}${sec1Hex.length > 36 ? '…' : ''}</div></div>`;
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">SEC16 (legacy) slot 2 @ 0x023A</div><div class="v">${sec2Hex.slice(0,36)}${sec2Hex.length > 36 ? '…' : ''}</div></div>`;
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">SEC16 legacy status</div><div class="v">${sec16Status}</div></div>`;
    if (parsed.extendedSec16 && parsed.extendedSec16.present) {
      const ext1Hex = bytesToHex(parsed.extendedSec16.slot1);
      const extStatus = parsed.extendedSec16.virgin ? 'VIRGIN' : parsed.extendedSec16.match ? 'MATCH' : 'MISMATCH';
      body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">SEC16 (2020+ extended) @ 0x050E</div><div class="v">${ext1Hex.slice(0,36)}${ext1Hex.length > 36 ? '…' : ''}</div></div>`;
      body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Extended SEC16 status</div><div class="v">${extStatus} · 2018+ module variant</div></div>`;
    }
    body += `<div class="kv"><div class="k">Keys programmed</div><div class="v">${parsed.keyCount} slot${parsed.keyCount === 1 ? '' : 's'} populated</div></div>`;
  }

  return `
    <div class="mod-card ${s.cls}">
      <div class="ttl">${title}<span class="badge ${s.cls}">${s.label}</span></div>
      ${body}
    </div>
  `;
}

function computeMatchBanner() {
  const b = state.bcm.parsed, r = state.rfh.parsed;
  if (!b || !r || !b.ok || !r.ok) return '';
  if (b.vin === r.vin) {
    return `<div class="match-banner ok">✓ VIN MATCH — BCM and RFHUB both carry <strong style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;margin:0 4px;letter-spacing:2px;">${b.vin}</strong> · modules are already paired</div>`;
  }
  return `<div class="match-banner mismatch">✗ VIN MISMATCH — BCM has <strong style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;margin:0 4px;letter-spacing:2px;">${b.vin}</strong> but RFHUB has <strong style="font-family:'JetBrains Mono',monospace;margin:0 4px;letter-spacing:2px;">${r.vin}</strong> · sync required before key programming</div>`;
}

function updateUI() {
  const b = state.bcm.parsed, r = state.rfh.parsed;
  const loaded = (state.bcm.bytes ? 1 : 0) + (state.rfh.bytes ? 1 : 0);
  $('loadCount').textContent = `${loaded} / 2`;

  if (loaded === 0) {
    $('inspectCard').classList.add('hidden');
    $('actionsCard').classList.add('hidden');
    return;
  }

  $('inspectCard').classList.remove('hidden');
  $('matchBanner').innerHTML = computeMatchBanner();
  $('resultsGrid').innerHTML = (b ? renderModCard(b, 'bcm') : '<div class="mod-card" style="opacity:0.4;">BCM not loaded</div>')
                              + (r ? renderModCard(r, 'rfh') : '<div class="mod-card" style="opacity:0.4;">RFHUB not loaded</div>');

  if (loaded === 2 && b.ok && r.ok) {
    $('actionsCard').classList.remove('hidden');
    renderActions();
  } else {
    $('actionsCard').classList.add('hidden');
  }
}

function renderActions() {
  const b = state.bcm.parsed, r = state.rfh.parsed;
  const tv = $('targetVin').value.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9]/g, '');
  const tvOk = tv.length === 17 && VIN_RE.test(tv);

  const actions = [
    {
      id: 'rfh-to-bcm',
      title: '➡ RFH VIN → BCM',
      desc: `Copy RFHUB VIN (${r.vin}) into BCM bin at all 4 slots. Downloads new BCM bin.`,
      enabled: r.ok,
      fn: () => doSync('rfh-to-bcm'),
    },
    {
      id: 'bcm-to-rfh',
      title: '⬅ BCM VIN → RFH',
      desc: `Copy BCM VIN (${b.vin}) into RFHUB bin (auto byte-reversed) at all 4 slots. Downloads new RFH bin.`,
      enabled: b.ok,
      fn: () => doSync('bcm-to-rfh'),
    },
    {
      id: 'target-both',
      title: '🎯 TARGET VIN → BOTH',
      desc: tvOk 
        ? `Write ${tv} into BOTH modules. Downloads both new bins.`
        : 'Enter a 17-char target VIN above to enable.',
      enabled: tvOk,
      fn: () => doSync('target-both'),
    },
  ];

  $('actionsRow').innerHTML = actions.map(a => `
    <button class="act" ${a.enabled ? '' : 'disabled'} data-action="${a.id}">
      <div class="atitle">${a.title} <span class="arrow">›</span></div>
      <div class="adesc">${a.desc}</div>
    </button>
  `).join('');

  for (const a of actions) {
    const el = document.querySelector(`[data-action="${a.id}"]`);
    if (el && a.enabled) el.addEventListener('click', a.fn);
  }
}

function downloadBin(bytes, filename) {
  const blob = new Blob([bytes], { type: 'application/octet-stream' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  a.download = filename;
  document.body.appendChild(a);
  a.click();
  document.body.removeChild(a);
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
}

function timestamp() {
  const d = new Date();
  const pad = n => n.toString().padStart(2, '0');
  return `${d.getFullYear()}${pad(d.getMonth()+1)}${pad(d.getDate())}_${pad(d.getHours())}${pad(d.getMinutes())}${pad(d.getSeconds())}`;
}

function doSync(action) {
  const b = state.bcm.parsed, r = state.rfh.parsed;
  const virginize = $('virginizeChk').checked;
  const ts = timestamp();

  log(`=== SYNC ACTION: ${action} ===`, 'info');
  if (virginize) log('Virginize: ON — will wipe RFH SEC16 slots', 'warn');

  try {
    if (action === 'rfh-to-bcm') {
      log(`Writing VIN ${r.vin} to BCM bin…`, 'info');
      const res = writeBcmVin(state.bcm.bytes, r.vin);
      log(`  BCM: patched ${res.patched} VIN slot(s)`, 'ok');
      const name = `BCM_SYNCED_${r.vin}_${ts}.bin`;
      downloadBin(res.bytes, name);
      log(`  Downloaded: ${name}`, 'ok');
      // Also regenerate RFH if virginize is on
      if (virginize) {
        const rres = writeRfhVin(state.rfh.bytes, r.vin, true);
        log(`  RFHUB: re-wrote VIN + wiped ${rres.sec16Wiped} legacy SEC16 slot(s)`, 'ok');
        if (rres.extendedWiped) log(`  RFHUB: also wiped 2020+ extended SEC16 region`, 'warn');
        const rname = `RFH_VIRGIN_${r.vin}_${ts}.bin`;
        downloadBin(rres.bytes, rname);
        log(`  Downloaded: ${rname}`, 'ok');
      }
    } else if (action === 'bcm-to-rfh') {
      log(`Writing VIN ${b.vin} to RFHUB bin (byte-reversed)…`, 'info');
      const res = writeRfhVin(state.rfh.bytes, b.vin, virginize);
      log(`  RFHUB: patched ${res.patched} VIN slot(s)`, 'ok');
      if (virginize) log(`  RFHUB: wiped ${res.sec16Wiped} SEC16 slot(s)`, 'warn');
      const name = virginize 
        ? `RFH_SYNCED_VIRGIN_${b.vin}_${ts}.bin`
        : `RFH_SYNCED_${b.vin}_${ts}.bin`;
      downloadBin(res.bytes, name);
      log(`  Downloaded: ${name}`, 'ok');
    } else if (action === 'target-both') {
      const tv = $('targetVin').value.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9]/g, '');
      log(`Writing target VIN ${tv} to BOTH modules…`, 'info');
      const bres = writeBcmVin(state.bcm.bytes, tv);
      log(`  BCM: patched ${bres.patched} VIN slot(s)`, 'ok');
      const bname = `BCM_SYNCED_${tv}_${ts}.bin`;
      downloadBin(bres.bytes, bname);
      log(`  Downloaded: ${bname}`, 'ok');
      const rres = writeRfhVin(state.rfh.bytes, tv, virginize);
      log(`  RFHUB: patched ${rres.patched} VIN slot(s)`, 'ok');
      if (virginize) {
        log(`  RFHUB: wiped ${rres.sec16Wiped} legacy SEC16 slot(s)`, 'warn');
        if (rres.extendedWiped) log(`  RFHUB: also wiped 2020+ extended SEC16 region`, 'warn');
      }
      const rname = virginize
        ? `RFH_SYNCED_VIRGIN_${tv}_${ts}.bin`
        : `RFH_SYNCED_${tv}_${ts}.bin`;
      downloadBin(rres.bytes, rname);
      log(`  Downloaded: ${rname}`, 'ok');
    }
    log('✓ Sync complete. Check your downloads folder.', 'ok');
    log('Reminder: flash the BIN files to their respective modules via your J2534/BDM tool, then power-cycle the bench for 30s to let the modules handshake.', 'muted');
  } catch (e) {
    log(`✗ Error: ${e.message}`, 'err');
  }
}

/* Init */
setupDrop('dropBcm', 'fileBcm', 'bcm');
setupDrop('dropRfh', 'fileRfh', 'rfh');

$('targetVin').addEventListener('input', e => {
  const v = e.target.value.toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-HJ-NPR-Z0-9]/g, '').slice(0, 17);
  e.target.value = v;
  const c = $('vinCount');
  c.textContent = `${v.length} / 17`;
  c.classList.toggle('ok', v.length === 17);
  renderActions();
});

$('virginizeChk').addEventListener('change', () => {
  log(`Virginize option: ${$('virginizeChk').checked ? 'ON' : 'OFF'}`, 'muted');
});

log('SRT Lab Sync Tool ready. Drop BCM and RFHUB .bin files to begin.', 'info');
log('Supported: Huntsville Continental BCM (68525720 / 68277389 family) + Yazaki FCM RFHUB (AA30712804 family)', 'muted');
log('Verified offsets across 2016 LD Scat Pack and 2017 LX Scat Pack dumps.', 'muted');

</script>
</body>
</html>

pause

@echo off
REM ===========================================================================
REM  Launches the debug proxy on port 8766.
REM
REM  PREREQUISITES:
REM    - j2534_bridge.py must be running on port 8765
REM      (use SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat to start it)
REM
REM  HOW TO USE:
REM    1. Run this bat. A Python window stays open logging traffic.
REM    2. In the browser UI, change the bridge URL from :8765 to :8766
REM       (look for a bridge URL input field on the AUTEL SGW tab or J2534 tab)
REM    3. Click scan in the browser.
REM    4. Watch THIS window — every request the browser sends is logged.
REM    5. Copy the log and paste it.
REM
REM  This tells us EXACTLY what the JSX is sending that fails.
REM ===========================================================================

set "PY=C:\Users\GOATMEZ\AppData\Local\Programs\Python\Python311-32\python.exe"
if not exist "%PY%" (
    echo [X] 32-bit Python not found at %PY%
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM --- Copy the proxy script if not in Downloads already ---
set "SRC_URL_NOTE=download debug_proxy.py from Claude and place it in Downloads"
if not exist "%USERPROFILE%\Downloads\debug_proxy.py" (
    echo.
    echo [X] %USERPROFILE%\Downloads\debug_proxy.py not found
    echo     %SRC_URL_NOTE%
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM --- Launch the proxy ---
echo Launching debug proxy on port 8766...
echo Bridge must be running on 8765 already.
echo.
"%PY%" "%USERPROFILE%\Downloads\debug_proxy.py"
pause

@echo off

REM
REM  Self-contained: just run this file.

    echo [X] 32-bit Python missing at %PY%
    pause

)
if not exist "%DLL%" (

    taskkill /F /PID %%a >nul 2>&1
)

REM --- Decode base64 to actual .py file ---
echo [*] Decoding to %TARGET%...
certutil -decode "%B64FILE%" "%TARGET%" >nul
if errorlevel 1 (
    echo [X] certutil decode failed
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
del /q "%B64FILE%"

REM --- Verify patch is in the file ---
echo [*] Verifying patch...
findstr /c:"mask.TxFlags = ISO15765_FRAME_PAD" "%TARGET%" >nul
if errorlevel 1 (
    echo [X] Patch verification failed — mask.TxFlags not found
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
findstr /c:"patt.TxFlags = ISO15765_FRAME_PAD" "%TARGET%" >nul
if errorlevel 1 (
    echo [X] Patch verification failed — patt.TxFlags not found
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
echo [OK] Patch verified. Both mask.TxFlags and patt.TxFlags are set.

REM --- Launch bridge in new window ---
echo [*] Launching bridge...
start "SRT Lab J2534 Bridge" cmd /k ""%PY%" "%TARGET%" --dll "%DLL%""

REM --- Wait for bridge ---
echo [*] Waiting for bridge to come up...
set /a TRIES=0
:waitloop
set /a TRIES+=1
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul
curl -s -o nul http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/status
if %errorlevel%==0 goto bridge_up
if %TRIES% geq 20 (
    echo [X] Bridge didn't come up in 20s. Check its window.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
goto waitloop

:bridge_up
echo [OK] Bridge responding.
echo.

REM --- STEP 1: Connect CAN channel ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 1/4 - Connect CAN (ISO15765 / 500 kbps)
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/connect ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"protocol\":6,\"flags\":0,\"baudrate\":500000}" > "%TEMP%\step1.txt" 2>&1
type "%TEMP%\step1.txt"
echo.
echo.

REM --- STEP 2: Install flow control filter for ECM (0x7E0 / 0x7E8) ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 2/4 - Install flow-control filter (ECM 0x7E0/0x7E8)
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/setfilter ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":2016,\"rxId\":2024}" > "%TEMP%\step2.txt" 2>&1
type "%TEMP%\step2.txt"
echo.
echo.

REM --- STEP 3: Send UDS 22 F1 90 (Read VIN) ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 3/4 - Send UDS 22 F1 90 (Read VIN) to ECM
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":2016,\"data\":\"22F190\"}" > "%TEMP%\step3.txt" 2>&1
type "%TEMP%\step3.txt"
echo.
echo.

REM --- STEP 4: Read response ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 4/4 - Read ECM reply
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"timeoutMs\":3000}" > "%TEMP%\step4.txt" 2>&1
type "%TEMP%\step4.txt"
echo.
echo.

REM --- STEP 5: Start tester-present periodic so body modules stay awake ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 5/5 - Start tester-present periodic (3E 80 on 0x7DF, 1000ms)
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/startperiodic ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":2015,\"data\":\"3E80\",\"intervalMs\":1000}" > "%TEMP%\step5.txt" 2>&1
type "%TEMP%\step5.txt"
echo.
echo.

echo ================================================================
echo  DONE. Interpretation:
echo    STEP 1 → channelConnected:true    = CAN up
echo    STEP 2 → ok:true, filterId:...    = BRIDGE FIX CONFIRMED
echo    STEP 3 → ok:true (nothing else)   = TX accepted
echo    STEP 4 → data:"000007E862F190..." = ECM answered (SUCCESS)
echo         or msg:null                   = bus silent (wiring/terminator)
echo ================================================================
pause


################################################################
# FILE: SRTLAB_HELLCAT_PROBE.bat
# SIZE: 4672 bytes
################################################################

@echo off
REM ===========================================================================
REM  SRT Lab — 2021 Hellcat ECM safe probe
REM
REM  READ-ONLY. Identifies the ECM variant and captures a seed for analysis.
REM  Does NOT attempt to unlock. Does NOT burn key attempts.
REM
REM  Requires bridge from SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat still running.
REM
REM  Steps:
REM    A) Filter on 0x7E0/0x7E8
REM    B) 10 03 extended session (harmless, resets on power cycle)
REM    C) 22 F1 90 — VIN (confirm it's responding)
REM    D) 22 F1 91 — hardware number
REM    E) 22 F1 93 — hardware version
REM    F) 22 F1 94 — software number
REM    G) 22 F1 95 — software version
REM    H) 22 F1 8C — ECU serial
REM    I) 22 F1 A0 — vehicle config
REM    J) 22 F1 11 — ECU core type
REM    K) 10 02 programming session (no write yet, just sees if it'll enter)
REM    L) 27 01 — single seed request (no key sent, does NOT burn attempts
REM       on GPEC-family modules — they only count attempts on 27 02)
REM ===========================================================================

setlocal enabledelayedexpansion

set "PORT=8765"
set "LOG=%USERPROFILE%\Desktop\hellcat_probe_log.txt"
set "TX=2016"
set "RX=2024"

if exist "%LOG%" del "%LOG%"

echo ================================================================
echo  2021 Hellcat ECM — Safe Probe (READ ONLY, no key writes)
echo  Target: 0x7E0 / 0x7E8
echo ================================================================

curl -s -o nul http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/status
if not %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo [X] Bridge is NOT running. Run SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat first.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM --- Install filter (may already exist from previous run, that's OK) ---
echo [A] Installing filter...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/setfilter ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"rxId\":%RX%}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === FILTER ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"

REM --- Enter extended session ---
echo [B] 10 03 extended session...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"1003\"}" >nul
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":1500}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === 10 03 SESSION ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"

REM --- Probe each identity DID ---
call :probe_did F190 "VIN"
call :probe_did F191 "Hardware number"
call :probe_did F193 "Hardware version"
call :probe_did F194 "Software number"
call :probe_did F195 "Software version"
call :probe_did F18C "ECU serial number"
call :probe_did F1A0 "Vehicle config"
call :probe_did F111 "ECU core type"
call :probe_did F192 "Supplier ECU hw number"
call :probe_did F197 "System name / engine type"

REM --- Try entering programming session ---
echo [K] 10 02 programming session...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"1002\"}" >nul
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":2000}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === 10 02 PROGRAMMING SESSION ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"

REM --- Request a single seed (no key sent — doesn't burn attempts) ---
echo [L] 27 01 seed request (no key will be sent)...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"2701\"}" >nul
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":2000}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === 27 01 SEED REQUEST ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  Probe complete. Log: %LOG%
echo.
echo  Opening log in Notepad for copy/paste...
echo ================================================================
notepad "%LOG%"
pause
exit /b 0


:probe_did
set "DID=%~1"
set "LABEL=%~2"
echo [DID %DID%] %LABEL%...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"22%DID%\"}" >nul
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":2000}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === DID %DID% (%LABEL%) ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"
goto :eof


################################################################
# FILE: SRTLAB_HELLCAT_SEED.bat
# SIZE: 3051 bytes
################################################################

@echo off
REM ===========================================================================
REM  SRT Lab — Hellcat seed capture (clean, drained, timed properly)
REM
REM  Purpose: capture ONE real seed from the ECM so we can identify the
REM  correct seed-key algorithm. Does NOT send a key. Safe to run repeatedly.
REM ===========================================================================

setlocal enabledelayedexpansion

set "PORT=8765"
set "LOG=%USERPROFILE%\Desktop\hellcat_seed_log.txt"
set "TX=2016"
set "RX=2024"

if exist "%LOG%" del "%LOG%"

echo ================================================================
echo  Hellcat ECM seed capture - clean run
echo ================================================================

curl -s -o nul http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/status
if not %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo [X] Bridge not running. Run SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat first.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM --- Install filter (might already exist, that's fine) ---
echo [1] Filter...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/setfilter ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"rxId\":%RX%}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.

REM --- DRAIN any stale messages ---
echo [2] Draining old messages...
:drain1
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":100}" > "%TEMP%\d.txt"
findstr /c:"\"msg\": null" "%TEMP%\d.txt" >nul
if errorlevel 1 (
    type "%TEMP%\d.txt"
    echo   drained one
    goto drain1
)
echo   queue empty.
echo.

REM --- Extended session ---
echo [3] 10 03 session...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"1003\"}" >nul
timeout /t 2 /nobreak >nul

REM read until we get a real message or 3 empties
set /a TRY=0
:readsess
set /a TRY+=1
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":1500}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === SESSION 10 03 try %TRY% ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"
findstr /c:"\"msg\": null" "%TEMP%\p.txt" >nul
if not errorlevel 1 (
    if %TRY% lss 3 goto readsess
)
echo.

REM --- Now seed request ---
echo [4] 27 01 seed request...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"2701\"}" >nul
timeout /t 2 /nobreak >nul

REM read multiple times to catch the real seed response
echo.
echo [5] Reading back 5 times to capture response...
set /a COUNT=0
:readseed
set /a COUNT+=1
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":2000}" > "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo --- read %COUNT% ---
type "%TEMP%\p.txt"
echo.
echo === SEED READ %COUNT% ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\p.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"
if %COUNT% lss 5 goto readseed

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  Done. Opening log...
echo ================================================================
notepad "%LOG%"
pause


################################################################
# FILE: SRTLAB_SCAN_ALL.bat
# SIZE: 6009 bytes
################################################################

@echo off
REM ===========================================================================
REM  SRT Lab — SCAN ALL 49 FCA modules (the right way)
REM
REM  Unlike the broken UI scanner, this:
REM    - Installs a flow-control filter for EACH module's tx/rx pair
REM    - Sends 10 03 (session) then 22 F1 90 (read VIN)
REM    - Reads the reply
REM    - Reports every module that responds, positive or negative
REM
REM  Requires bridge from SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat still running.
REM ===========================================================================

setlocal enabledelayedexpansion

set "PORT=8765"
set "LOG=%USERPROFILE%\Desktop\srtlab_full_scan.txt"

if exist "%LOG%" del "%LOG%"

echo ================================================================ > "%LOG%"
echo  SRT Lab full J2534 scan >> "%LOG%"
echo  %DATE% %TIME% >> "%LOG%"
echo ================================================================ >> "%LOG%"
echo. >> "%LOG%"

echo ================================================================
echo  SRT Lab — scanning all 49 FCA module addresses
echo ================================================================

curl -s -o nul http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/status
if not %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo [X] Bridge not running. Run SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat first.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM -- All known FCA module TX/RX pairs --
REM    Format: NAME|TXdec|RXdec
REM    (decimal because cmd.exe math is a nightmare with hex)
call :probe "ECM"       2016 2024
call :probe "TCM"       2017 2025
call :probe "DTCM"      2018 2026
call :probe "BPCM"      2020 2028
call :probe "BCM_750"   1872 1880
call :probe "RFHUB_75F" 1887 1895
call :probe "ABS"       1888 1896
call :probe "IPC"       1856 1864
call :probe "ORC"       1880 1888
call :probe "ADCM"      1960 1968
call :probe "AMP"       1952 1960
call :probe "BSM"       1904 1912
call :probe "EPS"       1889 1897
call :probe "RADIO"     1906 1914
call :probe "HVAC"      1873 1881
call :probe "TPMS"      1874 1882
call :probe "SCCM"      1869 1901
call :probe "TIPM"      1868 1900
call :probe "SKREEM"    1882 1914
call :probe "BSM_RDR"   1905 1913
call :probe "TPMS_SENS" 1816 1824
call :probe "OCS_SENS"  1832 1840
call :probe "ECM_W7"    2021 2029
call :probe "TCM_W7"    2022 2030
call :probe "BCM_W7"    1970 1978
call :probe "BCM_DVIN"  1712 1720
call :probe "CCM"       1859 1891
call :probe "ADM"       1860 1892
call :probe "IPCM"      1862 1894
call :probe "DDM"       1864 1896
call :probe "PDM"       1865 1897
call :probe "EPS_ALT"   1866 1898
call :probe "SCCM_ALT"  1867 1899
call :probe "TPMS_ALT"  1870 1902
call :probe "BCM_742"   1858 1890
call :probe "IPC_745"   1861 1893
call :probe "RADIO_754" 1876 1884
call :probe "RADIO_753" 1875 1907
call :probe "BCM_SWARM" 1968 1976
call :probe "IPC_SWARM" 1824 1832
call :probe "RFHUB_SW"  1890 1898
call :probe "RADIO_SW"  2000 2008
call :probe "ORC_SWARM" 1840 1848
call :probe "REAR_AXLE" 1728 1736
call :probe "ACC"       1792 1800
call :probe "BCM_PNET"  1568 1576
call :probe "SKIM_PNET" 1857 1865
call :probe "RADIO_PN"  1992 2000
call :probe "HVAC_PNET" 1672 1680

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  Scan complete. Opening log in Notepad...
echo ================================================================
notepad "%LOG%"
pause
exit /b 0


:probe
set "NAME=%~1"
set "TX=%~2"
set "RX=%~3"

REM Compute hex for display (via python one-liner — small enough)
set "TXHEX=?"
set "RXHEX=?"
for /f "delims=" %%h in ('python -c "print('0x%%03X' %% %TX%)" 2^>nul') do set "TXHEX=%%h"
for /f "delims=" %%h in ('python -c "print('0x%%03X' %% %RX%)" 2^>nul') do set "RXHEX=%%h"

echo [%NAME%] TX=%TXHEX% RX=%RXHEX%...

REM Install filter (ignore error — means filter already exists from previous probe)
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/setfilter ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"rxId\":%RX%}" > nul 2>&1

REM Drain stale queue
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":100}" > nul 2>&1

REM Send 10 03 (extended session) — wakes module
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"1003\"}" > nul 2>&1
timeout /t 1 /nobreak > nul

REM Drain session response
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":500}" > nul 2>&1

REM Send 22 F1 90 (read VIN)
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"22F190\"}" > nul 2>&1
timeout /t 1 /nobreak > nul

REM Read response
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"timeoutMs\":1500}" > "%TEMP%\r.txt"

REM Parse — look for "data":"62f190..." (positive VIN response)
findstr /c:"62f190" "%TEMP%\r.txt" > nul
if %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo   ^> FOUND with VIN response
    echo [%NAME%] TX=%TXHEX% RX=%RXHEX% — FOUND, VIN response: >> "%LOG%"
    type "%TEMP%\r.txt" >> "%LOG%"
    echo. >> "%LOG%"
    goto :eof
)

REM Look for a 7f1x... (negative response — means module IS there, just rejected the read)
findstr /c:"\"data\": \"7f" "%TEMP%\r.txt" > nul
if %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo   ^> FOUND with NRC
    echo [%NAME%] TX=%TXHEX% RX=%RXHEX% — FOUND, NRC response: >> "%LOG%"
    type "%TEMP%\r.txt" >> "%LOG%"
    echo. >> "%LOG%"
    goto :eof
)

REM Look for any non-empty data field
findstr /c:"\"data\": \"\"" "%TEMP%\r.txt" > nul
if %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo   ^> silent
    echo [%NAME%] TX=%TXHEX% RX=%RXHEX% — silent ^(no real reply^) >> "%LOG%"
    goto :eof
)

findstr /c:"msg\": null" "%TEMP%\r.txt" > nul
if %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo   ^> silent
    echo [%NAME%] TX=%TXHEX% RX=%RXHEX% — silent ^(timeout, no reply^) >> "%LOG%"
    goto :eof
)

echo   ^> unknown response
echo [%NAME%] TX=%TXHEX% RX=%RXHEX% — unknown response: >> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\r.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo. >> "%LOG%"

goto :eof


################################################################
# FILE: SRTLAB_WAKE_AND_READ.bat
# SIZE: 3780 bytes
################################################################

@echo off
REM ===========================================================================
REM  SRT Lab — wake the ECM, then read VIN
REM
REM  Assumes the bridge is already running from SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat.
REM  Don't re-launch the bridge — just run this second-stage test.
REM
REM  Sequence:
REM    A) 10 03 — enter extended diagnostic session
REM    B) 3E 80 — tester present (suppress response), keeps module awake
REM    C) 22 F1 90 — read VIN
REM    D) Read the reply
REM ===========================================================================

set "PORT=8765"
set "LOG=%USERPROFILE%\Desktop\srtlab_wake_log.txt"

echo ================================================================
echo  ECM Wake-and-Read Test
echo ================================================================

REM --- Check bridge is running ---
curl -s -o nul http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/status
if not %errorlevel%==0 (
    echo [X] Bridge is NOT running. Run SRTLAB_FIX_EVERYTHING.bat first.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM --- Try multiple ECM addresses in case 0x7E0 is wrong ---
REM  2017 Charger Scat Pack ECM is usually 0x7E0/0x7E8.
REM  Some GPEC2A ECMs use 0x7E5/0x7ED (ECM_W7).
REM  We try both.

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  ATTEMPT 1: ECM at 0x7E0/0x7E8 (standard)
echo ================================================================
call :try_ecm 2016 2024 "ECM_STD"

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  ATTEMPT 2: ECM at 0x7E5/0x7ED (ECM_W7 variant)
echo ================================================================
call :try_ecm 2021 2029 "ECM_W7"

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  All attempts complete. Log written to %LOG%
echo ================================================================
type "%LOG%" | more
notepad "%LOG%"
pause
exit /b 0


:try_ecm
REM  %1 = tx id decimal, %2 = rx id decimal, %3 = label
set "TX=%~1"
set "RX=%~2"
set "LABEL=%~3"

echo --- %LABEL%: tx=%TX% rx=%RX% ---

REM A) Install filter (new per target — old one stays but that's fine)
echo [%LABEL%] Installing filter tx=%TX% rx=%RX%...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/setfilter ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"rxId\":%RX%}" > "%TEMP%\f.txt"
type "%TEMP%\f.txt"
echo.
echo === %LABEL% FILTER ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\f.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"

REM B) Send 10 03 (extended diagnostic session)
echo [%LABEL%] Sending 10 03 (extended session)...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"1003\"}" > nul 2>&1

REM Give it a beat to reply
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul

REM Read any response
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"timeoutMs\":2000\}" > "%TEMP%\s.txt"
echo [%LABEL%] Session response:
type "%TEMP%\s.txt"
echo.
echo === %LABEL% SESSION 10 03 ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\s.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"

REM C) Drain queue
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"timeoutMs\":200}" > nul 2>&1

REM D) Send 22 F1 90 (read VIN)
echo [%LABEL%] Sending 22 F1 90 (read VIN)...
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":%TX%,\"data\":\"22F190\"}" > nul 2>&1

timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul

curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"timeoutMs\":3000}" > "%TEMP%\v.txt"
echo [%LABEL%] VIN read response:
type "%TEMP%\v.txt"
echo.
echo === %LABEL% VIN READ 22 F1 90 ===>> "%LOG%"
type "%TEMP%\v.txt" >> "%LOG%"
echo.>> "%LOG%"
echo.

goto :eof


################################################################
# FILE: run_bridge_and_test.bat
# SIZE: 5242 bytes
################################################################

@echo off
REM ============================================================================
REM  SRT Lab — J2534 bridge launcher and bench ECM smoke test
REM
REM  What this does:
REM   1. Kills any stale j2534_bridge.py process
REM   2. Starts the patched bridge in a new window with the correct DLL
REM   3. Waits for it to come up
REM   4. Runs four curl commands that prove end-to-end:
REM       - /connect brings up ISO15765 at 500k
REM       - /setfilter installs a flow-control filter for ECM (0x7E0/0x7E8)
REM       - /sendmsg sends UDS 22 F1 90 (Read VIN)
REM       - /readmsg pulls back whatever the ECM replied
REM   5. Prints the output of every step so you can see what happened
REM
REM  Pass the DLL path as arg 1 if yours is somewhere other than the default.
REM ============================================================================

setlocal enabledelayedexpansion

REM --- Config ---
set "PY=C:\Users\GOATMEZ\AppData\Local\Programs\Python\Python311-32\python.exe"
set "DLL=%~1"
if "%DLL%"=="" set "DLL=C:\Windows\SysWOW64\CFJW432.dll"
set "BRIDGE=%USERPROFILE%\Downloads\j2534_bridge.py"
set "PORT=8765"

echo.
echo ================================================================
echo  SRT Lab J2534 bridge launcher
echo ================================================================
echo  Python:  %PY%
echo  DLL:     %DLL%
echo  Bridge:  %BRIDGE%
echo  Port:    %PORT%
echo ================================================================
echo.

REM --- Sanity checks ---
if not exist "%PY%" (
    echo [X] 32-bit Python not found at %PY%
    echo     Install 32-bit Python 3.11 or edit the PY line at the top of this .bat
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
if not exist "%DLL%" (
    echo [X] DLL not found at %DLL%
    echo     Pass the full DLL path as the first argument, e.g.:
    echo         %~nx0 "C:\Windows\SysWOW64\CFJW432.dll"
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
if not exist "%BRIDGE%" (
    echo [X] Bridge script not found at %BRIDGE%
    echo     Copy the patched j2534_bridge.py into %USERPROFILE%\Downloads first.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)

REM --- Kill any previous instance on this port ---
echo [*] Stopping any existing bridge on port %PORT%...
for /f "tokens=5" %%a in ('netstat -aon ^| findstr ":%PORT%" ^| findstr "LISTENING"') do (
    echo     Killing pid %%a
    taskkill /F /PID %%a >nul 2>&1
)
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul

REM --- Launch the bridge in a new window so its output stays visible ---
echo [*] Starting bridge in new window...
start "SRT Lab J2534 Bridge" cmd /k ""%PY%" "%BRIDGE%" --dll "%DLL%""

REM --- Wait for the bridge to respond ---
echo [*] Waiting for bridge to come up...
set /a TRIES=0
:waitloop
set /a TRIES+=1
timeout /t 1 /nobreak >nul
curl -s -o nul -w "" http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/status
if %errorlevel%==0 goto bridge_up
if %TRIES% geq 15 (
    echo [X] Bridge did not come up within 15 seconds.
    echo     Check the "SRT Lab J2534 Bridge" window for errors.
    pause
    exit /b 1
)
goto waitloop

:bridge_up
echo [OK] Bridge is up.
echo.

REM --- Step 1: /connect ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 1/4 - Connect CAN channel (ISO15765 at 500kbps)
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/connect ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"protocol\":6,\"flags\":0,\"baudrate\":500000}"
echo.
echo.

REM --- Step 2: /setfilter ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 2/4 - Install flow-control filter for ECM (0x7E0 / 0x7E8)
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/setfilter ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":2016,\"rxId\":2024}"
echo.
echo.

REM --- Step 3: /sendmsg ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 3/4 - Send UDS 22 F1 90 (Read VIN)
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/sendmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"txId\":2016,\"data\":\"22F190\"}"
echo.
echo.

REM --- Step 4: /readmsg ---
echo ================================================================
echo  STEP 4/4 - Read the ECM reply
echo ================================================================
curl -s -X POST http://127.0.0.1:%PORT%/readmsg ^
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" ^
    -d "{\"timeoutMs\":3000}"
echo.
echo.

echo ================================================================
echo  Test sequence complete.
echo ================================================================
echo.
echo  INTERPRETATION:
echo    STEP 1 should return channelConnected:true
echo    STEP 2 should return ok:true with a filterId number
echo    STEP 3 should return ok:true (nothing else)
echo    STEP 4 should return a msg object with data starting "000007E862F190..."
echo           (that's the ECM's 62 F1 90 ^<VIN bytes^> response)
echo.
echo  If STEP 4 returns msg:null, the ECM is not responding on 0x7E0/0x7E8.
echo  If STEP 2 returns ERR_INVALID_MSG, the bridge patch didn't apply.
echo.
echo  The bridge window is still running. Close it when you're done.
echo.
pause
